id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_body" class="ajax__tab_body ajax__scroll_vert"> <div id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlFeatures" class="ajax__tab_panel" style="visibility: visible;"> <div class="Features"> <span id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlFeatures_ProductFeatureDesc"><h2><font style="color: #000000;">CZ&nbsp;</font></h2> <h2><font style="color: #000000;">Model 04140 CZ 557 Sporter Bolt 30-06 Springfield 20.5" Walnut Stock</font></h2> <pre><pre>The 557 is a departure from the Mauser-style bolt found on CZ's 550 models.<br>Instead, it has a short extractor and plunger-style ejector for smooth<br>operation and enhanced ejection. The short extractor or "push feed" system<br>also makes it easier to single load the rifle, which many shooters prefer<br>for range work. The receiver is machined from steel billet and has CZ's<br>integral 19mm dovetails for mounting a scope. Equipped with a 2-position<br>safety, the bolt can be cycled while the rifle is on 'safe.' To top it off,<br>it comes with a fully adjustable trigger that allows the owner to tune<br>weight, creep and over-travel to their liking. Clad in an American-style<br>walnut stock, the action is paired with CZ's legendary cold hammer-forged,<br>factory-lapped barrel. The resulting rifle is destined to become a<br>treasured hunting companion. Both short and standard action lengths are<br>available depending on chambering. </pre> <br></pre></span></div> </div><div id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_TabSpecifications" class="ajax__tab_panel" style="display:none;visibility:hidden;"> <div class="Features"> <span id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_TabSpecifications_ProductsSpecifications"><ul><li>Category : Rifles</li><li>Action : Bolt</li><li>Caliber : 30-06 Springfield</li><li>Barrel Length : 20.5"</li><li>Capacity : 5+1</li><li>Trigger : Adjustable</li><li>Safety : Manual</li><li>OAL : 41"</li><li>Weight : 7.3 lbs</li><li>Stock Description : Walnut</li><li>Metal Finish : Black</li></ul></span></div> </div> </div> </div> </div> </div> </div> <!-- Right Content --> <div class="RightContent" itemprop="offers" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Offer"> <div id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_UpdPnlOrderingOptions"> <div class="OrderingOptions"> <div id="Attributes"> </div> <div id="Add-Ons" align="right"> </div> <!--Information : If you change Add-Ons <div> tag ID [EX:<div ID ="Add-Ons">] , then you need to update that name in this javascript [File:"thumbnailviewer.js"] on line no :43 and 111.
